LONG ISLAND.; LONG ISLAND. A STREET FRACAS.--A well-known physician of Brooklyn was attacked by 0 citizen Wednesday evening, on North-Fourth-street, who avowed his intention of having the Doctor's "heart's blood," The parties clinched and had a lively time of it for a few minutes, when they were separated by the bystanders and before any serious damage had been done. The assallant then made a speech to the crowd, and stated that the Doctor had reduced his daughter.

Article 12 -- No Title
Petty Roguery.; To the Editor of the New-York Times: Permit me to call the attention of your City readers to a species of roguery, on a small scale, which is daily perpetrated at--not in--the City Post-Office. Near the window, where stamps are sold, may be seen well-dressed boys, from 10 to 14 years of age, selling Post-Office Stamps.
